Roman',serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Item&#160;8.01 Other Events.</span></div><div style="margin-top:5pt;text-indent:27pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">On October 30, 2025, Netflix, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) announced that the Company&#8217;s Board of Directors approved a ten-for-one forward stock split (the &#8220;Stock Split&#8221;) of the Company&#8217;s issued common stock to be effected through the filing of an amendment to the Company&#8217;s Amended and Restated Certificate of Incorporation (the &#8220;Amendment&#8221;) with the Secretary of the State of Delaware. The Amendment will also proportionately increase the number of shares of the Company&#8217;s authorized common stock. As a result of the Stock Split, each shareholder of record as of the close of trading on November 10, 2025 (the &#8220;Record Date&#8221;) will receive, after the close of trading on November 14, 2025, nine additional shares for every share held on the Record Date. Trading is expected to begin on a split-adjusted basis on November 17, 2025.</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-indent:27pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">LOS GATOS, Calif., October 30, 2025 - </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Netflix, Inc. (Nasdaq&#58; NFLX) announced today that its Board of Directors has approved a ten-for-one forward stock split of the Company&#8217;s common stock. The split will be effected through an amendment to the Company&#8217;s Amended and Restated Certificate of Incorporation. The purpose of the stock split is to reset the market price of the Company&#8217;s common stock to a range that will be more accessible to employees who participate in the Company&#8217;s stock option program. Each shareholder of record as of the close of trading on Monday, November 10, 2025 (the &#8220;record date&#8221;) will receive, after the close of trading on Friday, November 14, 2025, nine additional shares for every share held on the record date. Trading is expected to begin on a split-adjusted basis at market open on Monday, November 17, 2025. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">About Netflix, Inc.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Netflix is one of the world's leading entertainment services with over 300 million paid memberships in over 190 countries enjoying TV series, films and games across a wide variety of genres and languages. Members can play, pause and resume watching as much as they want, anytime, anywhere, and can change their plans at any time.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><table style="border-collapse:collapse;display:inline-table;margin-bottom:5pt;vertical-align:text-bottom;width:100.000%"><tr><td style="width:1.0%"></td><td style="width:22.876%"></td><td style="width:0.1%"></td><td style="width:1.0%"></td><td style="width:74.924%"></td><td style="width:0.1%"></td></tr><tr style="height:33pt"><td colspan="3" style="padding:0 1pt"></td><td colspan="3" style="padding:0 1pt"></td></tr></table></div></div></div></body></html>

var Show={};Show.LastAR=null,Show.showAR=function(a,r,w){if(Show.LastAR)Show.hideAR();var e=a;while(e&&e.nodeName!='TABLE')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e||e.nodeName!='TABLE'){var ref=((window)?w.document:document).getElementById(r);if(ref){e=ref.cloneNode(!0);
e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
e.style.display=d;if(a.textContent){a.textContent=p+a.textContent.substring(1)}else{a.innerText=p+a.innerText.substring(1)}}}
